msg:Let's talk about the location first. It's really good. It's by the Suzhou River, next to the Zhapu Road Bridge, a great photo spot. Many people take photos there at night. Behind it is the Postal Museum. Walk a little further to the Huangpu River. On the left is the North Bund, and on the right is the Bund. It's not too far to take a taxi anywhere. The room facilities are very new, with a view of the Suzhou River and the Oriental Pearl Tower in the distance. It's very clean. I stayed for two days in a row and came back to clean up in the morning and afternoon. The breakfast is delicious and exquisite. There is a buffet and you can also order meals. The small wontons are made and cooked, and the steamed pork ribs and shrimp dumplings and small steamed buns are very popular with children.

Check-in: I booked through other channels before, but I didn't expect to encounter problems. A manager in the hotel lobby told me that I needed to handle the cancellation of other channels myself. The answer was very polite and official, but her expression betrayed her! But another manager took the initiative to help me solve the problem. Although I didn't remember the name, I was still very grateful and tried to help me upgrade the next day under such tight housing supply. I really express my gratitude again!
Environment: City Walk is the best choice, and it is very convenient to go anywhere around. The internal environment is also very good. It is troublesome to bring two children. Toiletries and fences are provided! I didn't book a river view terrace, so I could only feel it slowly on the sixth floor and during breakfast time.
Service: Except for the small episodes of check-in that vary from person to person, the staff in other lines are great, which is what a hotel of this level should be like! Special thanks to Manager Kelvin for helping to coordinate the moving of luggage and taking care of the children and their emotions. I am very grateful.

The hotel has an excellent geographical location. I have stayed in almost all the hotels with beautiful river views on both sides of the Huangpu River, but most of them are high-rise, and it is impossible to walk out of the room to the outdoors, let alone such a large terrace. Bulgari is perfect for guests like me who go to Shanghai on business trips. There are only a few such resources on both sides of the Huangpu River. There may be a small terrace for smoking in Shanghai Seagull Hotel, and another island hotel that has not been digested through OTA channels. There may be very few other similar resources. Your hotel has not noticed and used such scarce resources well. It is said that the occupancy rate during the stay is more than 70%, and the terrace rooms on the side of the three-piece landscape are almost all dark (empty rooms). Why? The service is not up to standard. It cannot be said that if it is sold for more than 4,000 yuan per room, it is expensive. It can only be said that customers who usually stay at this price will not stay at your home again. Due to limited space, a detailed analysis will be sent to the emails of the hotel and the group's responsible personnel. Here is a brief introduction to the second point of the Black Swan. Each room in the hotel is equipped with a butler cabinet, but your hotel may not know how to use it, or the guests may not know how to use it. As a result, during the stay, the waiter entered the room many times to deliver supplies, and even broke into the room at 0:00 in the morning. After negotiation, the butler cabinet was still not used the next day. This is like a beautiful male peacock with gorgeous feathers, but it dares not spread its feathers. It does not know how to promote its own advantages, guide it, and does not understand the psychology of consumers. The third point of the Black Swan is that the iPads equipped in the hotel rooms can directly control room equipment such as curtains, TVs, and lights. This is the first time in so many years. What's even more strange is that they called me back at midnight the next night and said they were looking for the engineering depar**ent. I feel that the employees work very hard, but the managers have no awareness, direction, or requirements, and the employees can only meet basic customer needs. The future market must be polarized. Your hotel's own conditions limit it to more than 100 rooms, and the self-service requirements are not improved. The services of hotels that opened earlier with more than 700 rooms are similar, and the operating income will definitely not be ideal. There will definitely be no night shift switchboard. The large terrace in the room is definitely worth the price. The terrace is very wide. Although the floor is not high, the view is very good and unobstructed. Standing on it, with a three-piece suit on your left hand, you are facing the old buildings of Huangpu. On your right hand, you can see the Guangguang Building Group. The Suzhou River meanders in front of you, as if you are in Shanghai. The real center. It's especially beautiful when the lights are on at night.
The interior circulation of the room progresses layer by layer. The innermost side is a bathroom and shower room equipped with a washlet, and a rare small bottle of supplies. There is a small TV in front of the bathtub, equipped with bath salts; there are double basins, and the supplies are equipped with a beautiful Paper box storage. The minibar and coffee machine are hidden in the double-door door of the bedroom, which is unique. Except for drinking water, tea bags and coffee, all extra charges are required. The two meter wide bed is very comfortable. Once the door is closed and the blackout curtain is lowered, you can completely isolate yourself from the noise outside.
Breakfast is served at coffee on the second floor, a combination of buffet and a la carte. There are not many buffet stalls, but fortunately the a la carte menu is pretty good.
The cool atrium is buzzing with activity.
The gym is open to residents 24 hours a day. It faces the Suzhou River and Lujiazui during training, and the apples provided are quite delicious.
The 28-degree constant-temperature swimming pool, the light blue water color is very beautiful, and the design of the starry sky roof is very special; the soaking pool connected to the swimming pool is in the turret facing Lujiazui on the Bund. There is no one else in the afternoon, so you can enjoy it alone, which is very comfortable.
We were given a delicious cake on our anniversary. Will come again on important days in the future.

1: I arrived at the hotel at 11 o'clock on the day of check-in. There are two staff members at the front desk of the hotel. One male staff member checks in on another man. I heard them say, hello, we have upgraded your room today.
The person who checked me in was a staff member wearing a red skirt with no expression on his face, and asked me directly whose name I used to make the reservation? (There is no polite way of saying hello here). During the process of going through the formalities, I also tried to ask if it is possible to upgrade the room, and the other party said, no, the room is full. And told me that I can only check in at 3 pm, and now the room has not been refunded. I figured since it's supposed to be the hotel's policy, I'll just have to wait. Because it was raining that day, I waited at a coffee shop near the hotel. At 3 and 15 in the afternoon, I called the hotel and said that the room was still not cleaned up. At around 3:45 in the afternoon, I called and said that one room was cleaned up, because the room that was originally prepared for me was too dirty to be cleaned up, so give it to me Upgraded, it was a very polite person who seemed to be the front desk manager, well, upgrade me! Thank you, it was a pleasure meeting the manager when I was given my key card, thank you. I got back to the hotel at 4:30pm. After arriving at the room, I called the front desk to ask for the luggage to be delivered. Because it was stored at that time, the young man at the concierge put the two large luggage directly at the door and left. He was not going to send them into the room at all.
2: Because the package bought by Ctrip includes a 1,000 yuan voucher, I want to make an appoin**ent for afternoon tea the next day. I call the switchboard to ask if I need to make a reservation. The front desk said yes, and told me that there are floors 1 and 6. choose. I went to the terrace on the 6th floor of this hotel 4 years ago, so I knew the environment on the 6th floor was very good, so I asked the switchboard to transfer to the restaurant on the 6th floor. 4 They don‚Äôt have afternoon tea on the 6th floor, and then she made an appoin**ent for me on the 1st floor, and I also made it clear that I wanted to find a seat by the window, and the time was set at 3:30 pm. On the 19th of the next day, I took my children out to play after breakfast. I returned to the hotel at 2 o'clock thinking about taking a rest, and then went to the afternoon tea. I deliberately passed by the afternoon tea place and asked if I had booked a seat. A man said yes Yes, I asked again that it was indeed a seat by the window. Just as I was about to go back to the room, a female staff member, probably wearing a gray work suit, frowned, and seemed a little impatient to remind me that you can come here earlier because it is raining, I don‚Äôt know, what she said meant What? What is your expression? I told her that my time was 3:30.

Several things were connected together, I complained, and the cleaning attendant came over after a while and said sorry, she didn't see it, and I didn't understand what she didn't see. The manager on duty also called me very politely and apologized.
At this time, we were not in the mood to go to afternoon tea. We took a rest after taking a shower and left the hotel to find something to eat elsewhere. Because I don't want to see their service staff in the lobby bar.

It's not my style to touch it.

5: These are basically the feelings of staying for two days, no exaggeration, no right or wrong, just a statement. The benevolent see benevolence. But overall, Bellagio's services and facilities are very comfortable, worthy of recommendation and five-star praise
